gap-1 empty:hidden first:pt-[3px]"><div class="markdown prose w-full break-words dark:prose-invert light"><p>To run a Rust file, you need to use <strong>Cargo</strong> (Rust’s package manager) or the <code>rustc</code> compiler directly. Here’s how:</p><h3>1. Running a Rust File with Cargo</h3><p>Cargo is the recommended way to compile and run Rust projects because it handles dependencies and project structure easily.</p><ol><li><p><strong>Initialize a New Cargo Project</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">cargo new project_name
<span class="hljs-built_in">cd</span> project_name
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Write Code</strong>: Edit the <code>src/main.rs</code> file to add your code.</p></li><li><p><strong>Run the Code</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">cargo run
</code></div></div></pre><p>This will build and run your Rust project. Cargo compiles the project, resolves dependencies, and caches the build files in the <code>target</code> directory.</p></li></ol><h3>2. Running a Single Rust File with <code>rustc</code></h3><p>If you only have a single Rust file and don’t need a full Cargo project, you can use the <code>rustc</code> command directly:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Compile the File</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">rustc filename.rs
</code></div></div></pre><p>This will create an executable in the same directory.</p></li><li><p><strong>Run the Executable</strong>:</p><ul><li>On <strong>Linux/macOS</strong>:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">./filename
</code></div></div></pre></li><li>On <strong>Windows</strong>:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">filename.exe
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul></li></ol><h3>Example</h3><p>If you have a file named <code>hello.rs</code> with the following code:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">rust</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-rust"><span class="hljs-keyword">fn</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span>() {
    <span class="hljs-built_in">println!</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Hello, Rust!"</span>);
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>You can run it either by:</p><ol><li><p>Using Cargo:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">cargo new hello_project
<span class="hljs-built_in">cd</span> hello_project
<span class="hljs-comment"># Move hello.rs content into src/main.rs, then</span>
cargo run
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Using <code>rustc</code>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">rustc hello.rs
./hello    <span class="hljs-comment"># On Windows: hello.exe</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><h3>Notes</h3><ul><li>Cargo is better for managing dependencies and is generally recommended for larger projects.</li><li>For quick tests and small scripts, <code>rustc</code> is simpler if you don’t need a full project structure.</li></ul></div></div></div></div><div class="mb-2 flex gap-3 empty:hidden -ml-2"><div class="items-center justify-start ---

# 🚀 Rust for Data Engineering

Welcome to **Rust for Data Engineering**! This repository demonstrates the power of Rust for data engineering tasks such as ETL, data transformation, and real-time data processing. Rust combines speed, memory safety, and concurrency, making it perfect for robust, high-performance data pipelines.

## 📑 Table of Contents
- [✨ Introduction](#introduction)
- [🎯 Features](#features)
- [⚙️ Getting Started](#getting-started)
  - [Installation](#installation)
  - [Running with Docker](#running-with-docker)
  - [Configuration &amp; Hardware](#configuration--hardware)
- [📚 Modules](#modules)
- [🚀 Usage](#usage)
- [📁 Examples](#examples)
- [🤝 Contributing](#contributing)
- [❓ FAQ](#faq)

- [📌 Anything Else](#anything-else)

## ✨ Introduction
Rust’s reputation as a safe, high-performance systems language is well-deserved. This project explores Rust’s strengths in data engineering, covering ETL pipelines, real-time data processing, and complex data transformations with libraries like **Polars**, **Serde**, and **Tokio**.

## 🎯 Features
- 🚀 **Efficient ETL Pipelines**: Ingest, transform, and load data into destinations like MongoDB or S3.
- 🧩 **Data Transformation**: Utilize **Polars** for fast, powerful data manipulation.
- 🔥 **Real-Time Processing**: Real-time ingestion with Redis and Kafka.
- 🧵 **Concurrency**: Leverage async tasks to handle high data loads with ease.

## ⚙️ Getting Started

### 💻 Installation

Rust can be installed across different operating systems as described below:

#### From the Official Site
1. Head to [Rust's Official Website](https://www.rust-lang.org/) and download the installer.
2. Follow the prompts to set up Rust, Cargo, and related tools.
3. Confirm installation by running:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   rustc --version</code></pre>

#### Quick Install via Shell
For any Unix-like system (Linux or macOS), you can install Rust directly using the Rustup installer script:
<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
curl --proto '=https' --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh</code></pre>

#### Installation by OS

- **Windows**:
   1. Download and install Rust using [rustup-init.exe](https://static.rust-lang.org/rustup/dist/x86_64-pc-windows-msvc/rustup-init.exe).
   2. Open PowerShell or Command Prompt and run:
      <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>powershell
      rustup-init.exe</code></pre>
   3. After installation, close and reopen your terminal to ensure Cargo (Rust’s package manager) is added to your PATH.
   
- **macOS**:
   1. You can use the shell command above or install via [Homebrew](https://brew.sh/):
      <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
      brew install rustup
      rustup-init</code></pre>
   2. To update Rust and Cargo paths, add this to your shell profile:
      <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
      export PATH="$HOME/.cargo/bin:$PATH"</code></pre>
   
- **Linux**:
   - Most Linux distributions support Rust installation with the shell command. If you prefer using a package manager:
      - **Ubuntu/Debian**:
         <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
         sudo apt update
         sudo apt install rustc</code></pre>
      - **Fedora**:
         <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
         sudo dnf install rust</code></pre>
   - To ensure Cargo is in your path, add:
     <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
     export PATH="$HOME/.cargo/bin:$PATH"</code></pre>

### Running with Docker
If you prefer Docker, you can use the official Rust image:

1. Pull the Rust image from Docker Hub:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   docker pull rust</code></pre>
2. Run Rust commands in a container:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   docker run -it --rm rust:latest</code></pre>
3. To build and run your Rust projects in Docker, mount the project directory:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   docker run -v $(pwd):/usr/src/myapp -w /usr/src/myapp rust cargo build</code></pre>

### Updating Rust
Keep Rust up to date with:
<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
rustup update</code></pre>

### ⚙️ Configuration &amp; Hardware

- **Memory Requirements**: Rust is efficient, but at least 4GB of RAM is recommended for data processing tasks.
- **CPU Compatibility**: Ensure your system supports modern instructions (e.g., SSE4) for data processing with Polars.
- **Environment Variables**: Add Cargo to your PATH, typically done by Rustup during installation.

## 📚 Modules

1. **Data Ingestion (<code>src/data_ingestion</code>)** 🗃️
   - Ingest data from files, APIs, and databases using **Serde**.

2. **Data Transformation (<code>src/data_transformation</code>)** 🔄
   - Transform data with filtering, joining, and aggregation using **Polars**.

3. **Data Loading (<code>src/data_loading</code>)** 🗄️
   - Load data into MongoDB, Redis, and S3 with async I/O.

4. **Real-Time Processing (<code>src/real_time_processing</code>)** ⏱️
   - Stream and process data with Kafka and Redis.

5. **Utilities (<code>src/utils</code>)** 🛠️
   - Helper functions for logging, error handling, and configurations.

## 🚀 Usage

### Running a Basic ETL Pipeline
<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
cargo run --example etl_pipeline</code></pre>

### Real-Time Data Processing
<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
cargo run --example real_time_processing</code></pre>

## 📁 Examples

- **ETL Pipeline Example**: Ingests and transforms CSV data, then loads it to MongoDB.
- **Real-Time Processing Example**: Streams data through Kafka and processes it.
- **Data Transformation Example**: Performs aggregations with Polars.

## 🤝 Contributing
1. Fork the repo and create a new branch.
2. Commit your changes with tests.
3. Submit a pull request!

## ❓ FAQ

### Important Things to Remember While Using Rust
- **Ownership and Borrowing**: Rust’s strict ownership model helps avoid memory errors. Check out the [Rust Ownership documentation](https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/ch04-00-understanding-ownership.html).
- **Concurrency with Tokio**: Use the <code>#[tokio::main]</code> attribute for async functions and wrap I/O tasks in <code>tokio::spawn</code>.
- **Error Handling**: Rust uses <code>Result</code> and <code>Option</code> types for error handling. [Anyhow](https://docs.rs/anyhow/latest/anyhow/) and [ThisError](https://docs.rs/thiserror/latest/thiserror/) are also popular for structured error handling.
- **Macros and Pattern Matching**: Rust’s macros like <code>match</code> and <code>if let</code> provide powerful control flows and are integral in clean error handling.

### What if I Get Stuck?
- Rust’s official book and documentation are invaluable resources:
  - [The Rust Programming Language Book](https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/)
  - [Rust by Example](https://doc.rust-lang.org/rust-by-example/)
  - [Rust Cookbook](https://rust-lang-nursery.github.io/rust-cookbook/)
- **YouTube Tutorials**:
  - [Rust for Beginners by Traversy Media](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=zF34dRivLOw)
  - [Learn Rust Programming - Full Course by freeCodeCamp](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=MsocPEZBd-M)
  - [Rust Crash Course by Fireship](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Oxjw8bK3U_0)

## 💬 Community &amp; Resources

- **[Rust Documentation](https://doc.rust-lang.org/)** 📘
- **[Rust Discord Community](https://discord.gg/rust-lang)** 💬
- **[Rust Reddit](https://www.reddit.com/r/rust/)** 👥
- **[Rust Users Forum](https://users.rust-lang.org/)** 📢

## 📈 Rust's Journey and Why It Matters for Data Engineers

### Rust's Development Over the Years
Since its initial release, Rust has grown rapidly, earning a reputation for performance and safety, and consistently topping developer surveys for most-loved language. As of now, Rust has reached a maturity level that makes it an ideal choice for system-level and high-performance applications, with key improvements in error handling, async programming, and stable libraries.

### Why Rust Is a Game-Changer for Data Engineers
Rust’s focus on performance, memory safety, and zero-cost abstractions makes it uniquely suited for data engineering:
1. **Concurrency and Parallelism**: Rust’s async model and Tokio library make it easy to handle large-scale data tasks.
2. **Reliability**: Rust’s strict compile-time checks minimize runtime errors, crucial for data integrity.
3. **Scalability**: Data engineers can build pipelines that handle increasing data loads with minimal memory footprint.

For data engineers who want to push the limits of efficiency and reliability, Rust offers tools to build pipelines that are faster, safer, and more scalable than traditional languages.

## 📌 Anything Else

Data is growing exponentially, and handling it demands both speed and precision. --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> for</span><span style="--animation-count: 19; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Data</span><span style="--animation-count: 20; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Engineers</span></a></li><li><a rel="noopener" href="https://chatgpt.com/c/672a8a24-4984-8001-ad6f-e81ba9e9325c#anything-else" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 13; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">📌 Anything</span><span style="--animation-count: 14; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Else</span></a></li></ul><h2>✨ Introduction</h2><p>Rust’s reputation as a safe, high-performance systems language is well-deserved. This project explores Rust’s strengths in data engineering, covering ETL pipelines, real-time data processing, and complex data transformations with libraries like <strong>Polars</strong>, <strong>Serde</strong>, and <strong>Tokio</strong>.</p><h2>🎯 Features</h2><ul><li>🚀 <strong>Efficient ETL Pipelines</strong>: Ingest, transform, and load data into destinations like MongoDB or S3.</li><li>🧩 <strong>Data Transformation</strong>: Utilize <strong>Polars</strong> for fast, powerful data manipulation.</li><li>🔥 <strong>Real-Time Processing</strong>: Real-time ingestion with Redis and Kafka.</li><li>🧵 <strong>Concurrency</strong>: Leverage async tasks to handle high data loads with ease.</li></ul><h2>⚙️ Getting Started</h2><h3>💻 Installation</h3><p>Rust can be installed across different operating systems as described below:</p><h4>From the Official Site</h4><ol><li>Head to <a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://www.rust-lang.org/" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 14; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">Rust's</span><span style="--animation-count: 15; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Official</span><span style="--animation-count: 16; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Website</span></a> and download the installer.</li><li>Follow the prompts to set up Rust, Cargo, and related tools.</li><li>Confirm installation by running:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">rustc --version
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><h4>Quick Install via Shell</h4><p>For any Unix-like system (Linux or macOS), you can install Rust directly using the Rustup installer script:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">curl --proto <span class="hljs-string">'=https'</span> --tlsv1.2 -sSf https://sh.rustup.rs | sh
</code></div></div></pre><h4>Installation by OS</h4><ul><li><strong>Windows</strong>:<ol><li>Download and install Rust using <a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://static.rust-lang.org/rustup/dist/x86_64-pc-windows-msvc/rustup-init.exe" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); </code></div></div></pre></li></ul></li></ul><h3>Running with Docker</h3><p>If you prefer Docker, you can use the official Rust image:</p><ol><li>Pull the Rust image from Docker Hub:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">docker pull rust
</code></div></div></pre></li><li>Run Rust commands in a container:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">docker run -it --<span class="hljs-built_in">rm</span> rust:latest
</code></div></div></pre></li><li>To build and run your Rust projects in Docker, mount the project directory:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">docker run -v $(<span class="hljs-built_in">pwd</span>):/usr/src/myapp -w /usr/src/myapp rust cargo build
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><h3>Updating Rust</h3><p>Keep Rust up to date with:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">rustup update
</code></div></div></pre><h3>⚙️ Configuration &amp; Hardware</h3><ul><li><strong>Memory Requirements</strong>: Rust is efficient, but at least 4GB of RAM is recommended for data processing tasks.</li><li><strong>CPU Compatibility</strong>: Ensure your system supports modern instructions (e.g., SSE4) for data processing with Polars.</li><li><strong>Environment Variables</strong>: Add Cargo to your PATH, typically done by Rustup during installation.</li></ul><h2>📚 Modules</h2><ol><li><p><strong>Data Ingestion (<code>src/data_ingestion</code>)</strong> 🗃️</p><ul><li>Ingest data from files, APIs, and databases using <strong>Serde</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Data Transformation (<code>src/data_transformation</code>)</strong> 🔄</p><ul><li>Transform data with filtering, joining, and aggregation using <strong>Polars</strong>.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Data Loading (<code>src/data_loading</code>)</strong> 🗄️</p><ul><li>Load data into MongoDB, Redis, and S3 with async I/O.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Real-Time Processing (<code>src/real_time_processing</code>)</strong> ⏱️</p><ul><li>Stream and process data with Kafka and Redis.</li></ul></li><li><p><strong>Utilities (<code>src/utils</code>)</strong> 🛠️</p><ul><li>Helper functions for logging, error handling, and configurations.</li></ul></li></ol><h2>🚀 Usage</h2><h3>Running a Basic ETL Pipeline</h3><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative </code></div></div></pre><h2>📁 Examples</h2><ul><li><strong>ETL Pipeline Example</strong>: Ingests and transforms CSV data, then loads it to MongoDB.</li><li><strong>Real-Time Processing Example</strong>: Streams data through Kafka and processes it.</li><li><strong>Data Transformation Example</strong>: Performs aggregations with Polars.</li></ul><h2>🤝 Contributing</h2><ol><li>Fork the repo and create a new branch.</li><li>Commit your changes with tests.</li><li>Submit a pull request!</li></ol><h2>❓ FAQ</h2><h3>Important Things to Remember While Using Rust</h3><ul><li><strong>Ownership and Borrowing</strong>: Rust’s strict ownership model helps avoid memory errors. Check out the <a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/ch04-00-understanding-ownership.html" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 17; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">Rust</span><span style="--animation-count: 18; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Ownership</span><span style="--animation-count: 19; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> documentation</span></a>.</li><li><strong>Concurrency with Tokio</strong>: Use the <code>#[tokio::main]</code> attribute for async functions and wrap I/O tasks in <code>tokio::spawn</code>.</li><li><strong>Error Handling</strong>: Rust uses <code>Result</code> and <code>Option</code> types for error handling. <a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://docs.rs/anyhow/latest/anyhow/" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 18; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">Anyhow</span></a> and <a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://docs.rs/thiserror/latest/thiserror/" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 19; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">ThisError</span></a> are also popular for structured error handling.</li><li><strong>Macros and Pattern Matching</strong>: Rust’s macros like <code>match</code> and <code>if let</code> provide powerful control flows and are integral in clean error handling.</li></ul><h3>What if I Get Stuck?</h3><ul><li>Rust’s official book and documentation are invaluable resources:<ul><li><a rel="noopener" target="_new" href="https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Forum</span></a></strong> 📢</li></ul><h2>📈 Rust's Journey and Why It Matters for Data Engineers</h2><h3>Rust's Development Over the Years</h3><p>Since its initial release, Rust has grown rapidly, earning a reputation for performance and safety, and consistently topping developer surveys for most-loved language. As of now, Rust has reached a maturity level that makes it an ideal choice for system-level and high-performance applications, with key improvements in error handling, async programming, and stable libraries.</p><h3>Why Rust Is a Game-Changer for Data Engineers</h3><p>Rust’s focus on performance, memory safety, and zero-cost abstractions makes it uniquely suited for data engineering:</p><ol><li><strong>Concurrency and Parallelism</strong>: Rust’s async model and Tokio library make it easy to handle large-scale data tasks.</li><li><strong>Reliability</strong>: Rust’s strict compile-time checks minimize runtime errors, crucial for data integrity.</li><li><strong>Scalability</strong>: Data engineers can build pipelines that handle increasing data loads with minimal memory footprint.</li></ol><p>For data engineers who want to push the limits of efficiency and reliability, Rust offers tools to build pipelines that are faster, safer, and more scalable than traditional languages.</p><h2>📌 Anything Else</h2><p>Data is growing exponentially, and handling it demands both speed and precision. Rust’s ability to create efficient, reliable systems makes it an ideal choice</p></div></div></div></div><div class="mb-2 flex gap-3 empty:hidden -ml-2"><div class="items-center justify-start py-[18px] px-3 md:px-4 w-full md:px-5 lg:px-4 xl:px-5"><div class="mx-auto flex flex-1 gap-4 text-base md:gap-5 lg:gap-6 md:max-w-3xl lg:max-w-[40rem] xl:max-w-[48rem]"><div class="group/conversation-turn relative flex w-full min-w-0 flex-col"><div class="flex-col gap-1 md:gap-3"><div class="flex max-w-full flex-col flex-grow"><div data-message-author-role="user" data-message-id="aaa28a9a-4f39-43f7-94e3-47e0d30d63a3" dir="auto" class="min-h-8 text-message flex w-full flex-col items-end gap-2 whitespace-normal break-words [.text-message+&amp;]:mt-5"><div class="flex w-full flex-col gap-1 empty:hidden items-end rtl:items-start"><div class="relative max-w-[70%] rounded-3xl px-5 py-2.5 bg-[#f4f4f4] dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><div class="whitespace-pre-wrap">add ths- To run a Rust file, you need to use **Cargo** (Rust’s package manager) or the <code>rustc</code> compiler directly. Here’s how:

### 1. Running a Rust File with Cargo

Cargo is the recommended way to compile and run Rust projects because it handles dependencies and project structure easily.

1. **Initialize a New Cargo Project**:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   cargo new project_name
   cd project_name</code></pre>

2. **Write Code**: Edit the <code>src/main.rs</code> file to add your code.

3. **Run the Code**:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   cargo run</code></pre>

   This will build and run your Rust project. Cargo compiles the project, resolves dependencies, and caches the build files in the <code>target</code> directory.

### 2. Running a Single Rust File with <code>rustc</code>

If you only have a single Rust file and don’t need a full Cargo project, you can use the <code>rustc</code> command directly:

1. **Compile the File**:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   rustc filename.rs</code></pre>

   This will create an executable in the same directory.

2. **Run the Executable**:
   - On **Linux/macOS**:
     <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
     ./filename</code></pre>
   - On **Windows**:
     <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
     filename.exe</code></pre>

### Example
If you have a file named <code>hello.rs</code> with the following code:
<pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>rust
fn main() {
    println!("Hello, Rust!");
}</code></pre>

You can run it either by:
1. Using Cargo:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   cargo new hello_project
   cd hello_project
   # Move hello.rs content into src/main.rs, then
   cargo run</code></pre>

2. Using <code>rustc</code>:
   <pre class="overflow-x-auto"><code>bash
   rustc hello.rs
   ./hello    # On Windows: hello.exe</code></pre>

### Notes
- Cargo is better for managing dependencies and is generally recommended for larger projects.
- For quick tests and small scripts, <code>rustc</code> is simpler if you don’t need a full project structure.// to above readme file</div><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-full top-0 -mr-3.5 hidden Resources</span></a></li><li><a rel="noopener" href="https://chatgpt.com/c/672a8a24-4984-8001-ad6f-e81ba9e9325c#rusts-journey-and-why-it-matters-for-data-engineers" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> It</span><span style="--animation-count: 18; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Matters</span><span style="--animation-count: 19; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> for</span><span style="--animation-count: 20; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Data</span><span style="--animation-count: 21; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Engineers</span></a></li><li><a rel="noopener" href="https://chatgpt.com/c/672a8a24-4984-8001-ad6f-e81ba9e9325c#anything-else" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 84; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">📌 Anything</span><span style="--animation-count: 85; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Else</span></a></li></ul><h2>✨ Introduction</h2><p>Rust’s reputation as a safe, high-performance systems language is well-deserved. This project explores Rust’s strengths in data engineering, covering ETL pipelines, real-time data processing, and complex data transformations with libraries like <strong>Polars</strong>, <strong>Serde</strong>, and <strong>Tokio</strong>.</p><h2>🎯 Features</h2><ul><li>🚀 <strong>Efficient ETL Pipelines</strong>: Ingest, transform, and load data into destinations like MongoDB or S3.</li><li>🧩 <strong>Data Transformation</strong>: Utilize <strong>Polars</strong> for fast, powerful data manipulation.</li><li>🔥 <strong>Real-Time Processing</strong>: Real-time ingestion with Redis and Kafka.</li><li>🧵 <strong>Concurrency</strong>: Leverage async tasks to handle high data loads with ease.</li></ul><h2>⚙️ Getting Started</h2><h3>💻 Installation</h3><p>Rust can be installed across different operating systems. <a rel="noopener" href="https://chatgpt.com/c/672a8a24-4984-8001-ad6f-e81ba9e9325c#installation" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 85; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">See</span><span style="--animation-count: 86; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> installation</span><span style="--animation-count: 87; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> instructions</span><span style="--animation-count: 88; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> here.</span></a></p><h3>Running with Docker</h3><p>If you prefer Docker, you can use the official Rust image. <a rel="noopener" href="https://chatgpt.com/c/672a8a24-4984-8001-ad6f-e81ba9e9325c#running-with-docker" style="--streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-1); --animation-rate: var(--batch-play-rate-1);"><span style="--animation-count: 86; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);">See</span><span style="--animation-count: 87; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> Docker</span><span style="--animation-count: 88; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> instructions</span><span style="--animation-count: 89; --streaming-animation-state: var(--batch-play-state-2);"> here.</span></a></p><h3>⚙️ Configuration &amp; Hardware</h3><ul><li><strong>Memory Requirements</strong>: Rust is efficient, but at least 4GB of RAM is recommended for data processing tasks.</li><li><strong>CPU Compatibility</strong>: Ensure your system supports modern instructions (e.g., SSE4) for data processing with Polars.</li><li><strong>Environment Variables</strong>: Add Cargo to your PATH, typically done by Rustup during installation.</li></ul><h3>Running a Rust File</h3><p>To run a Rust file, you need to use <strong>Cargo</strong> (Rust’s package manager) or the <code>rustc</code> compiler directly. Here’s how:</p><h4>1. Running a Rust File with Cargo</h4><p>Cargo is the recommended way to compile and run Rust projects because it handles dependencies and project structure easily.</p><ol><li><p><strong>Initialize a New Cargo Project</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">cargo new project_name
<span class="hljs-built_in">cd</span> project_name
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p><strong>Write Code</strong>: Edit the <code>src/main.rs</code> file to add your code.</p></li><li><p><strong>Run the Code</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">cargo run
</code></div></div></pre><p>This will build and run your Rust project. Cargo compiles the project, resolves dependencies, and caches the build files in the <code>target</code> directory.</p></li></ol><h4>2. Running a Single Rust File with <code>rustc</code></h4><p>If you only have a single Rust file and don’t need a full Cargo project, you can use the <code>rustc</code> command directly:</p><ol><li><p><strong>Compile the File</strong>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">rustc filename.rs
</code></div></div></pre><p>This will create an executable in the same directory.</p></li><li><p><strong>Run the Executable</strong>:</p><ul><li>On <strong>Linux/macOS</strong>:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">./filename
</code></div></div></pre></li><li>On <strong>Windows</strong>:<pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">filename.exe
</code></div></div></pre></li></ul></li></ol><h4>Example</h4><p>If you have a file named <code>hello.rs</code> with the following code:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">rust</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-rust"><span class="hljs-keyword">fn</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span>() {
    <span class="hljs-built_in">println!</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"Hello, Rust!"</span>);
}
</code></div></div></pre><p>You can run it either by:</p><ol><li><p>Using Cargo:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">cargo new hello_project
<span class="hljs-built_in">cd</span> hello_project
<span class="hljs-comment"># Move hello.rs content into src/main.rs, then</span>
cargo run
</code></div></div></pre></li><li><p>Using <code>rustc</code>:</p><pre class="!overflow-visible"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-md border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-gray-950"><div class="flex items-center text-token-text-secondary px-4 py-2 text-xs font-sans justify-between rounded-t-md h-9 bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary select-none">bash</div><div class="sticky top-9 md:top-[5.75rem]"><div class="absolute bottom-0 right-2 flex h-9 items-center"><div class="flex items-center rounded bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary px-2 font-sans text-xs text-token-text-secondary dark:bg-token-main-surface-secondary"><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex gap-1 items-center select-none py-1"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-sm"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 5C7 3.34315 8.34315 2 10 2H19C20.6569 2 22 3.34315 22 5V14C22 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 19.5523 4 19 4H10C9.44772 4 9 4.44772 9 5V7ZM5 9C4.44772 9 4 9.44772 4 10V19C4 19.5523 4.44772 20 5 20H14C14.5523 20 15 19.5523 15 19V10C15 9.44772 14.5523 9 14 9H5Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy code</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="!whitespace-pre hljs language-bash">rustc hello.rs
./hello    <span class="hljs-comment"># On Windows: hello.exe</span>
</code></div></div></pre></li></ol><h4>Notes</h4><ul><li>Cargo is better for managing dependencies and is generally recommended for larger projects.</li><li>For quick tests and small scripts, <code>rustc</code> is simpler if you don’t need a full project structure.</li></ul><h2>📚 Modules</h2><p>... ### 1. Running a Rust File with Cargo

Cargo is the recommended way to compile and run Rust projects because it handles dependencies and project structure easily.

1. **Initialize a New Cargo Project**:
   ```bash
   cargo new project_name
   cd project_name
   ```

2. **Write Code**: Edit the `src/main.rs` file to add your code.

3. **Run the Code**:
   ```bash
   cargo run
   ```

   This will build and run your Rust project. Cargo compiles the project, resolves dependencies, and caches the build files in the `target` directory.

### 2. Running a Single Rust File with `rustc`

If you only have a single Rust file and don’t need a full Cargo project, you can use the `rustc` command directly:

1. **Compile the File**:
   ```bash
   rustc filename.rs
   ```

   This will create an executable in the same directory.

2. **Run the Executable**:
   - On **Linux/macOS**:
     ```bash
     ./filename
     ```
   - On **Windows**:
     ```bash
     filename.exe
     ```

### Example
If you have a file named `hello.rs` with the following code:
```rust
fn main() {
    println!("Hello, Rust!");
}
```

You can run it either by:
1. Using Cargo:
   ```bash
   cargo new hello_project
   cd hello_project
   # Move hello.rs content into src/main.rs, then
   cargo run
   ```

2. Using `rustc`:
   ```bash
   rustc hello.rs
   ./hello    # On Windows: hello.exe
   ```

### Notes
- Cargo is better for managing dependencies and is generally recommended for larger projects.
- For quick tests and small scripts, `rustc` is simpler if you don’t need a full project structure.

### ⚙️ Configuration & Hardware

- **Memory Requirements**: Rust is efficient, but at least 4GB of RAM is recommended for data processing tasks.
- **CPU Compatibility**: Ensure your system supports modern instructions (e.g., SSE4) for data processing with Polars.
- **Environment Variables**: Add Cargo to your PATH, typically done by Rustup during installation.

## 📚 Modules

1. **Data Ingestion (`src/data_ingestion`)** 🗃️
   - Ingest data from files, APIs, and databases using **Serde**.

2. **Data Transformation (`src/data_transformation`)** 🔄
   - Transform data with filtering, joining, and aggregation using **Polars**.

3. **Data Loading (`src/data_loading`)** 🗄️
   - Load data into MongoDB, Redis, and S3 with async I/O.

4. **Real-Time Processing (`src/real_time_processing`)** ⏱️
   - Stream and process data with Kafka and Redis.

5. **Utilities (`src/utils`)** 🛠️
   - Helper functions for logging, error handling, and configurations.

## 🚀 Usage

### Running a Basic ETL Pipeline
```bash
cargo run --example etl_pipeline
```

### Real-Time Data Processing
```bash
cargo run --example real_time_processing
```

## 📁 Examples

- **ETL Pipeline Example**: Ingests and transforms CSV data, then loads it to MongoDB.
- **Real-Time Processing Example**: Streams data through Kafka and processes it.
- **Data Transformation Example**: Performs aggregations with Polars.

## ❓ FAQ

### Important Things to Remember While Using Rust
- **Ownership and Borrowing**: Rust’s strict ownership model helps avoid memory errors. Check out the [Rust Ownership documentation](https://doc.rust-lang.org/book/ch04-00-understanding-ownership.html).
- **Concurrency with Tokio**: Use the `#[tokio::main]` attribute for async functions and wrap I/O tasks in `tokio::spawn`.
- **Error Handling**: Rust uses `Result` and `Option` types for error handling. [Anyhow](https://docs.rs/anyhow/latest/anyhow/) and [ThisError](https://docs.rs/thiserror/latest/thiserror/) are also popular for structured error handling.
- **Macros and Pattern Matching**: Rust’s macros like `match` and `if let` provide powerful control flows and are integral in clean error handling.

### What if I Get Stuck?

## 📈 Rust's Journey and Why It Matters for Data Engineers

### Rust's Development Over the Years
Since its initial release, Rust has grown rapidly, earning a reputation for performance and safety, and consistently topping developer surveys for most-loved language. As of now, Rust has reached a maturity level that makes it an ideal choice for system-level and high-performance applications, with key improvements in error handling, async programming, and stable libraries.

### Why Rust Is a Game-Changer for Data Engineers
Rust’s focus on performance, memory safety, and zero-cost abstractions makes it uniquely suited for data engineering:
1. **Concurrency and Parallelism**: Rust’s async model and Tokio library make it easy to handle large-scale data tasks.
2. **Reliability**: Rust’s strict compile-time checks minimize runtime errors, crucial for data integrity.
3. **Scalability**: Data engineers can build pipelines that handle increasing data loads with minimal memory footprint.

For data engineers who want to push the limits of efficiency and reliability, Rust offers tools to build pipelines that are faster, safer, and more scalable than traditional languages.
